entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', '--project', '/workspace', '/workspace/forge.py']

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_blueprint_list_uuid_tiebreak_when_created_at_and_name_collide(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str], data_dir: Path
    ) -> None:
        """List uses UUID as final tiebreaker when created_at and name are identical."""
        first = create_blueprint(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            name="uuid-tie-a",
            requirement_sets=[{"resource_type": "CPU", "resource_count": 1}],
        )
        second = create_blueprint(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            name="uuid-tie-b",
            requirement_sets=[{"resource_type": "GPU", "resource_count": 1}],
        )
        shared_timestamp = "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z"
        shared_name = "uuid-tie"
        store_path = data_dir / "blueprints.json"
        stored = json.loads(store_path.read_text())
        for row in stored:
            if row["uuid"] in {first["uuid"], second["uuid"]}:
                row["created_at"] = shared_timestamp
                row["name"] = shared_name
        store_path.write_text(
            json.dumps(stored, separators=(",", ":"), sort_keys=True)
        )
        listed = run_forge(entrypoint_argv, data_dir, ["blueprint", "list"])
>       payload = unwrap_collection(assert_success(listed), key="blueprints")

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_allocation_list_ordering(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str], data_dir: Path
    ) -> None:
        """List returns allocations sorted by created_at and uuid in ascending order."""
        create_blueprint(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            name="batch-a",
            requirement_sets=[{"resource_type": "gpu", "resource_count": 1}],
        )
        create_blueprint(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            name="batch-b",
            requirement_sets=[{"resource_type": "gpu", "resource_count": 1}],
        )
        run_forge(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            ["allocation", "create"],
            stdin_json={"blueprint_name": "batch-a"},
        )
        run_forge(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            ["allocation", "create"],

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_expansion_order_places_multiplied_entries_consecutively(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str], data_dir: Path
    ) -> None:
        """Create preserves requirement index order and keeps multiplied rows consecutive."""
        create_blueprint(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            name="ordering",
            requirement_sets=[
                {"resource_type": "gpu", "resource_count": 1},
                {
                    "resource_type": "fpga",
                    "resource_count": 1,

                },

            ],
        )

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_allocation_create_same_blueprint_twice_distinct_uuids(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str], data_dir: Path
    ) -> None:
        """Two create calls against the same blueprint produce independent allocations with unique UUIDs."""
        create_blueprint(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            name="reusable",
            requirement_sets=[{"resource_type": "gpu", "resource_count": 1}],
        )
        first = run_forge(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            ["allocation", "create"],
            stdin_json={"blueprint_name": "reusable"},
        )
        second = run_forge(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_list_order_tiebreaks(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str], data_dir: Path
    ) -> None:
        """List ordering applies uuid as tie-breaker when host/category/created_at match."""
        host = "node-tie"
        create_unit(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            category="zeta",
            manufacturer="acme",
            host=host,
            capacity=1,
        )
        create_unit(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            category="alpha",
            manufacturer="acme",
            host=host,
            capacity=1,
        )
        alpha_a = create_unit(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            category="alpha",
            manufacturer="acme-a",
            host=host,
            capacity=2,
        )
        alpha_b = create_unit(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            category="alpha",
            manufacturer="acme-b",
            host=host,
            capacity=2,
        )
        shared_timestamp = "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z"
        store_path = data_dir / "units.json"
        stored = json.loads(store_path.read_text())
        for row in stored:
            if row["uuid"] in {alpha_a["uuid"], alpha_b["uuid"]}:
                row["created_at"] = shared_timestamp
        store_path.write_text(
            json.dumps(stored, separators=(",", ":"), sort_keys=True)
        )
    
        listed = run_forge(
            entrypoint_argv, data_dir, ["unit", "list", "--host", host]
        )

data_dir = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_list_order_created_at_asc0/data')

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_list_order_created_at_ascending(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str], data_dir: Path
    ) -> None:
        """List orders by created_at ascending when host and category are identical."""
        host = "node-sort"
        category = "GPU"
        first = create_unit(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            category=category,
            host=host,
            capacity=1,
        )
        second = create_unit(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            category=category,
            host=host,
            capacity=2,
        )
    
        store_path = data_dir / "units.json"
        stored = json.loads(store_path.read_text())
        for row in stored:
            if row["uuid"] == first["uuid"]:
                row["created_at"] = "2024-01-01T00:00:02Z"
            elif row["uuid"] == second["uuid"]:
                row["created_at"] = "2024-01-01T00:00:01Z"
        store_path.write_text(
            json.dumps(stored, separators=(",", ":"), sort_keys=True)
        )
    
        listed = run_forge(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            ["unit", "list", "--host", host, "--category", category],
        )
>       payload = unwrap_collection(assert_success(listed), key="units")
                  ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

    def assert_error(
        result: subprocess.CompletedProcess[str],
        *,
        category: str,

        detail_contains: str | None = None,
        revision: str | None = None,
        has_revision: bool | None = None,
    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
        assert result.returncode == 1, (
            f"expected error exit code 1; stdout={result.stdout!r} "
            f"stderr={result.stderr!r}"
        )

        assert isinstance(payload, dict)

            data_dir,
            unit_uuid=unit_b["uuid"],

        )

        module_a = create_module(entrypoint_argv, data_dir, unit_uuid=unit["uuid"])
        module_b = create_module(entrypoint_argv, data_dir, unit_uuid=unit["uuid"])
    
        first = create_tag(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            module_uuid=module_a["uuid"],
            key="vendor",
            value="acme",
        )
        second = create_tag(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            module_uuid=module_b["uuid"],
            key="vendor",
            value="globex",
        )
        assert first["module_uuid"] != second["module_uuid"]
    
        duplicate = run_forge(
            entrypoint_argv,
            data_dir,
            ["tag", "create"],
            stdin_json={
                "module_uuid": module_a["uuid"],
                "key": "vendor",
                "value": "other",
            },
        )
        assert_error(
            duplicate, category="conflict", detail_contains=module_a["uuid"]
        )
    
        listed = run_forge(
            entrypoint_argv, data_dir, ["tag", "list", "--key", "vendor"]
        )
>       payload = unwrap_collection(assert_success(listed), key="tags")
                  ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
